msg:Came to Zhengzhou to watch a concert and chose Crowne Plaza Hotel. My husband went to school nearby and wanted to revisit the old place, so I chose Crowne Plaza near the school.
In general, it is very good and cost-effective. It is the most satisfactory Crowne Plaza I have ever stayed in. I must give it a big praise!

Facilities: Very new, very good, the room is very large and spacious, the sound insulation is very good, and the bedding is comfortable. The hotel is equipped with a swimming pool, which is very new and clean. It is so refreshing to take a hot bath after swimming every day!

Environment: The environment of the five-star hotel is nothing to say, it is very clean and comfortable. There are several large shopping malls around, which are actually no different from the City of David, so it is recommended to live here. Compared with the city center, the environment here is good and quiet, and it is not remote.

Service: The service is super good. It is the best service attitude of the Crowne Plaza I have ever stayed in. The staff is almost responsive, the front desk staff is particularly good, and Mr. Liang Zichao's meticulous service makes people feel at home.

Breakfast: Very delicious, with a wide variety of options, including Western-style muffins, waffles, various bread croissants, etc., as well as Henan-style spicy soup, steamed vegetables, mutton offal soup, stewed noodles, etc., and even more surprising is the Cantonese-style barbecued pork buns, custard buns, etc. After breakfast every day, I was not hungry until noon, and I couldn't eat enough~

In summary, I really recommend this hotel, the price-performance ratio is amazing! If I have the opportunity to go to Zhengzhou, I will definitely choose this hotel again!

I understand very well that the buffet operation is all for profit, but I beg you to consider the feelings of the guests staying in the hotel. The management of a five-star hotel should manage such things. You are a hotel, not a restaurant, so don't put the cart before the horse! Of course, still those few words, the attitude of the hotel is still very good, five-star standard! But I want to live conveniently, rest assured, and have food to eat. I don‚Äôt have this attitude. Continue to stay at Wanda Vista Hotel. As for Crowne Plaza hotels in other cities, I have to think about it!
